# DSMD
A dataset

You can get it on Baidu Netdisk: "https://pan.baidu.com/s/1AfBM7JjGd_hNTX_LyotiJQ?pwd=dsmd"

We are uploading the dataset to GitHub.


Here is the tree struct of DSMD.


DSMD

├── train

│   ├── images

│   └── labels

└── val

    ├── images

    └── labels
